## Usage and history

### Purpose

Genetic replication of an organism into a single or multiple duplicates[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Device)

:   "*Clones can think creatively. You will find that they are immensely superior to droids.*"
:   ―Lama Su, to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13)

**Cloning** was the process of duplicating an [organism](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") into one or many genetically identical individuals known as clones. During the [final years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), an [army](/wiki/Army "Army") of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") was grown on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"). Using the [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") as a template, the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") tampered with Fett's genetic structure to make his clones more docile. In addition, they were designed to grow at twice the rate of normal human aging, making the clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") ready for deployment in a [decade's](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") [time](/wiki/Time "Time"). At Fett's request, an unmodified clone—[Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett")—was created from his template and given to him to raise as his son.

During the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), Fett's clone [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") served in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") under [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") [leadership](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") until [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") called for the [destruction](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). The clones carried out their mandate due to their [programming](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip"), eliminating most of the [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") across [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), after which the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") was [formed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") by the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"). Shortly thereafter, the entire clone army was decommissioned and replaced by [birth-born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper").

The Empire ultimately [fell](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") to the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic") after the [Emperor's](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") [destruction](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"). However, Sidious managed to cheat [death](/wiki/Death "Death"). Through the combined use of cloning and the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") transferred his spirit to a new host that had been cloned from his original body. Though the transference had been a success, Sidious' new vessel suffered from rapid deterioration and was unable to contain the dark energy of his soul. His [followers](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist"), the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal"), experimented with Sidious' template in the hope of creating a more suitable vessel. Their efforts produced various [Strand-Casts](/wiki/Strand-Cast "Strand-Cast"), including [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") and multiple genetic copies of him, as well as a [modified clone](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan") that was healthy yet lacked Sidious' [connection](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") to [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). As such, the clone's only worth to Sidious lay in continuing the [Palpatine bloodline](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family") through more [natural means](/wiki/Miramir "Miramir"), resulting in the birth of [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") who, unlike her [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), was regarded as the ideal host for her grandfather's essence following [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo")'s [rejection](/wiki/Mission_to_Kef_Bir "Mission to Kef Bir") of the dark side.

## Overview[]

:   "*They are totally obedient, taking any order without question. We modified their genetic structure to make them less independent than the original host.*"
:   ―Lama Su[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13)

 [![Cloning was a science in which clones were grown from the template of a genetic donor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/CloneGrowthJar-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101201838) [![Cloning was a science in which clones were grown from the template of a genetic donor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/CloneGrowthJar-Aftermath.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220101201838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/CloneGrowthJar-Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20220101201838) 

Cloning was a science in which clones were grown from the template of a genetic donor.

 

Cloning was the scientific procedure of growing a clone from the [genetic template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") of a [living organism](/wiki/Species "Species").[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) The template's [DNA](/wiki/DNA "DNA") was the foundation for clones, which could number from at least one genetic copy to millions of specimens that shared the same face, voice, and even skills inherited from the original source.[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) The template's genetic code could be [altered through modifications](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") to the cloning process for various purposes, including growth acceleration and greater docility. Without alterations to the genome, a clone would be the exact duplicate of its template at the genetic level.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13)

The practice of cloning [humans](/wiki/Human "Human") was an imperfect science. In spite of the [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan")' efforts to perfect the art, it was still possible to discover the occasional genetic or physical defects in their specimens, producing both wanted and unwanted results.[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4)

 [![The Kaminoan government mass-produced millions of identical clone troopers for the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic.png/revision/latest?cb=20210619204924) [![The Kaminoan government mass-produced millions of identical clone troopers for the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210619204924)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bf/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic.png/revision/latest?cb=20210619204924) 

The Kaminoan government mass-produced millions of identical clone troopers for the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

Millions of clones could be grown from a single genetic sample, but only while it was viable. Over [time](/wiki/Time "Time") the sample would degrade. Therefore, cloners required regular access to the original source or donor in order to extract replacement samples. Otherwise a new host would have to be adopted to continue the cloning production. Clones were also considered mentally superior to [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid"). Their physical conditioning could be enhanced through technological augmentation, which, in the case of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), increased their chances of surviving against numerous endless waves of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid").[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4)

Clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") were created for the sole purpose of fighting; as such, they were afforded little respite. They were also capable of developing genuine resentment for their opponents, in particular the battle droids who they referred to by the derogatory slang "clankers." Some clones developed a habit for collecting droid parts as war trophies,[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) although this act was considered a sign of defectiveness or deviant behavior.[[14]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-14)

A clone's DNA could be modified in a way that made it impossible for the clone to disobey a specific order. This was accomplished by encoding a directive in the clone's biology.[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) [Strand-Casting](/wiki/Strand-Cast "Strand-Cast") was a modified form of the cloning process that resulted in the creation of a strandcast,[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) an "artificial genetic construct"[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) made from a hybrid of donated cells, some of which could be extracted from cloned tissue samples. This was the case with[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16) [Dathan](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan"),[[8]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-8) a strandcast whose composite genetic structure comprised the cells of various specimens, including the cloned DNA of the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious").[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16) The [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent") of [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") was, therefore, a non-identical clone of Sidious.[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17)

## History[]

### Fall of the Republic[]

:   "*Two hundred thousand units are ready, with a million more well on the way.*"
:   ―Lama Su[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13)

 [![The clone army was developed in Tipoca City and other cloning facilities throughout Kamino.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/Kamino_Tipoca_City.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080218034510) [![The clone army was developed in Tipoca City and other cloning facilities throughout Kamino.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/Kamino_Tipoca_City.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20080218034510)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/Kamino_Tipoca_City.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080218034510) 

The clone army was developed in Tipoca City and other cloning facilities throughout Kamino.

 

Though not the only practitioners of cloning in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), the [Kaminoan government](/wiki/Ruling_Council_(Kamino) "Ruling Council (Kamino)") turned its mass production of clones into a large-scale commercial enterprise.[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) It was through the Kaminoan cloning process that an [army](/wiki/Army "Army") was created for the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), almost ten [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), at the behest of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"). Under the leadership of [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su"), the Kaminoans utilized their cloning expertise to create[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) millions[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) of [genetically](/wiki/DNA "DNA")-engineered [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier") who would form the backbone of the new [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military").[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) The [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist") of Kamino, [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se"), was directly involved in the clone army's creation as one of its primary engineers.[[1]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-1)

Following the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of Sifo-Dyas,[[18]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas-18) the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") took control of his project and [hired](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") a human [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter"), [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett"), to serve as the army's clone template.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) Fett's genetic code served the foundation for millions of clone troopers who all shared the same face, voice, and combat prowess as their progenitor,[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) although they were also structurally modified at the genetic level to make them less independent[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) and more docile.[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) The first clones[[19]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-19) of the Jango Fett genotype[[11]](#cite_note-Fugitive-11) were designated as "generation one," and among their ranks was [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [CT-7567](/wiki/Rex "Rex")[[19]](#cite_note-Battle_Scars-19) of the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion").[[20]](#cite_note-CT-7567_DB-20)

 [![Clone troopers were modeled on a single genetic source, the human mercenary Jango Fett.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/Central_Armory.png/revision/latest?cb=20140802085546) [![Clone troopers were modeled on a single genetic source, the human mercenary Jango Fett.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/Central_Armory.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140802085546)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/Central_Armory.png/revision/latest?cb=20140802085546) 

Clone troopers were modeled on a single genetic source, the human mercenary Jango Fett.

 

Further genetic tampering caused Fett's clones to grow at twice the rate of the human [species](/wiki/Species "Species"), making them ready for deployment in a [decade's](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") time.[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) While the process of growing clone troopers was left to Kaminoan [scientists](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist"), the Sith took a more active role in their programming, having supplied their cloners with [behavioral modification biochips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip")[[1]](#cite_note-Conspiracy-1) to be implanted in the [brain](/wiki/Brain "Brain") of every clone at the earliest stage of their development. Portrayed as a structural inhibitor chip, they ostensibly made their hosts more docile and less aggressive than their template,[[11]](#cite_note-Fugitive-11) but their true purpose was to force the clones to obey [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66")—a secret protocol authorizing the immediate [extermination](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") as [enemies of the state](/wiki/Treason "Treason").[[21]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-21)

In addition to Fett's considerable [monetary](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") fee, the Kaminoans compensated him by creating a clone[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13)—codenamed [Alpha](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett")[[5]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-5)—that stood apart from the rest of his artificial progeny. Unlike the others, Alpha was an example of pure genetic replication and as such he was neither programmed for loyalty nor designed to grow at an accelerated rate. Fett took custody of the unmodified clone to raise as his son, granting him the name "Boba Fett."[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) Boba was not the only example of pure genetic replication, however. Another unmodified clone of Jango Fett was created, possessing first generation DNA, and was codenamed [Omega](/wiki/Omega "Omega").[[5]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-5) Omega was a human [female](/wiki/Gender "Gender") clone who served as Nala Se's medical [assistant](/wiki/Aide "Aide").[[22]](#cite_note-Aftermath-22)

### Clone Wars[]

:   "*I understand your concerns, Master Jedi. Ever since the unfortunate death of Jango Fett, we have had to stretch his DNA to produce more clones.*"
:   ―Lama Su, to Shaak Ti[[23]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-23)

 [![Led by the Jedi Knights, clones served as soldiers in the Grand Army of the Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/CodyObiWan.png/revision/latest?cb=20130202023207) [![Led by the Jedi Knights, clones served as soldiers in the Grand Army of the Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/CodyObiWan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130202023207)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/CodyObiWan.png/revision/latest?cb=20130202023207) 

Led by the Jedi Knights, clones served as soldiers in the Grand Army of the Republic.

 

The clone army's development had proceeded according to schedule as the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") entered its final [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day"). The Kaminoan [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital"), [Tipoca City](/wiki/Tipoca_City "Tipoca City"), housed tens of thousands of clones,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) while millions more were in development in facilities scattered across the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino").[[24]](#cite_note-CL-24) When [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") discovered the clone army, Su praised it as one of the finest ever produced by his people. As war became imminent, with thousands of secessionist [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") joining the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"), the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") empowered [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") Sheev Palpatine,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) secretly Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious,[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_III-25) to mobilize the clone troopers as the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic").[[21]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-21)

Clone troopers were the legal property of the Galactic Republic, although [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se "Nala Se")—one of the clones' main engineers—believed that the Kaminoan government still owned them.[[11]](#cite_note-Fugitive-11) Clones fought for the Republic on all battlefronts across the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") and were loyal to their [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") as well as Chancellor Palpatine.[[21]](#cite_note-Clone_Troopers-21) During the conflict, the Jedi oversaw the training of younger clones on Kamino. With a limited supply of genetic material from the late Jango, Lama Su was concerned that the new clones would be less effective as soldiers. He recommended the Jedi acquire a new template, but his Jedi liaison Master [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti "Shaak Ti"), advocated her support for the remaining Fett clones, particularly the [clone cadets](/wiki/Clone_cadet "Clone cadet") of [Domino Squad](/wiki/Domino_Squad "Domino Squad").[[23]](#cite_note-Clone_Cadets-23)

 [![The Separatists attacked Kamino with the aim of destroying or stealing the DNA record of Jango Fett.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/CloneTroopersDefendKamino-AT.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505070137) [![The Separatists attacked Kamino with the aim of destroying or stealing the DNA record of Jango Fett.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/CloneTroopersDefendKamino-AT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130505070137)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2a/CloneTroopersDefendKamino-AT.png/revision/latest?cb=20130505070137) 

The Separatists attacked Kamino with the aim of destroying or stealing the DNA record of Jango Fett.

 

Fett's genetic record was considered a military asset of the highest importance to the Republic's continued war effort. Knowing this, the Separatists sought to halt the production of new clones by invading Kamino, where the bounty hunter's genetic material was kept safe within the [Clone DNA room](/wiki/Clone_DNA_room "Clone DNA room")[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) of Tipoca City.[[26]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-26) Should the Confederacy have succeeded in destroying the room[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) or Fett's genetic material,[[26]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-26) clone trooper production would have come to a halt,[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) shifting the war in the Confederacy's favor. However, invasion commander and Kenobi’s rival, [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), also expressed interest in securing the Fett DNA for the Confederacy.[[26]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-26) Though the clone troopers were soldiers of the Republic, they harbored an affinity with the Kaminoan [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld"), which they viewed as their home as well. This collective sentiment motivated the clones to make every effort in pushing back against the Separatist invasion, ultimately winning the [Battle of Kamino](/wiki/Battle_of_Kamino "Battle of Kamino") through acts of bravery[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) and sacrifice.[[26]](#cite_note-ARC_Troopers-26)

As the war continued, the Senate broached the subject of buying more clones to augment the Grand Army's ranks. While [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") and other like-minded politicians advocated fiscal responsibility and a diplomatic solution to the war, others argued for increased military spending. Senator [Halle Burtoni](/wiki/Halle_Burtoni "Halle Burtoni") favored [legislation](/wiki/Politics "Politics") that would [deregulate](/wiki/Republic_financial_reform_bill "Republic financial reform bill") the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), thereby providing the Republic with new lines of credit to purchase more clone troopers from Burtoni's homeworld of Kamino.[[27]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-27) At the time of the [Siege of Saleucami](/wiki/Siege_of_Saleucami "Siege of Saleucami"), it was rumored the CIS was working on its own [clone-soldier program](/wiki/Unidentified_clone-soldier_program "Unidentified clone-soldier program") that could rival Kaminoan production in hidden laboratories on the planet [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami").[[28]](#cite_note-Battles_that_Changed-28)

### Age of the Empire[]

:   "*With the war at an end, the need for future clones is being questioned.*"  
    "*Our contracts stipulate the continued production.*"  
    "*Your contracts were with the Republic, which no longer exists.*"
:   ―Wilhuff Tarkin and Lama Su[[22]](#cite_note-Aftermath-22)

 [![The Imperial Army utilized clone troopers before turning to the recruitment of natural-born humans.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/YesCommander.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109223507) [![The Imperial Army utilized clone troopers before turning to the recruitment of natural-born humans.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/YesCommander.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220109223507)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4d/YesCommander.png/revision/latest?cb=20220109223507) 

The Imperial Army utilized clone troopers before turning to the recruitment of natural-born humans.

 

In the aftermath of the Clone Wars, Sidious [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the [First Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), reorganized from the Republic. During the early years of the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), the clone troopers that fought for the Republic became the first generation of [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper").[[29]](#cite_note-Stormtroopers-29) At first the clones continued to form the backbone of the army, and some troopers joined the ranks of the [Emperor's Royal Guard](/wiki/Emperor%27s_Royal_Guard "Emperor's Royal Guard"),[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) but to their own surprise the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") terminated the cloning operation on Kamino.[[30]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_2-30) The decision to phase the clones out of military service was influenced not only by their rapid aging process, but also the influx of non-clone humans who were inspired to enlist by Imperial [propaganda](/wiki/Propaganda "Propaganda").[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4)

The decision to terminate the production of clone troopers also came as a surprise to Prime Minister Su, who believed the Kaminoan government would continue to grow clones for the Republic after the Clone Wars ended. With the rise of the Empire, however, the contract between Kamino and the Republic was nullified. Following the [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor")'s announcement, his protege [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") and [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") was sent to Kamino—under the protection of [Imperial shock troopers](/wiki/Imperial_shock_trooper "Imperial shock trooper") of the [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard")—to assess the remaining clone units and determine whether there was a need to produce future clone troopers for the Empire. Su argued that the Empire needed more clones to maintain order throughout the galaxy, although Tarkin countered that was a service recruitment soldiers could provide at half the cost.[[22]](#cite_note-Aftermath-22)

 [![The Kaminoans regarded the introduction of conscripted soldiers in the Empire as a threat to their cloning operation.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/KaminoansandClones-WM.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116064255) [![The Kaminoans regarded the introduction of conscripted soldiers in the Empire as a threat to their cloning operation.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/KaminoansandClones-WM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220116064255)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9c/KaminoansandClones-WM.png/revision/latest?cb=20220116064255) 

The Kaminoans regarded the introduction of conscripted soldiers in the Empire as a threat to their cloning operation.

 

Su hoped to ensure the security of his people and their operation by convincing the Empire that the clones were indispensable. To that end, he sought to create a new breed of clones superior to the previous generations.[[31]](#cite_note-Replacements-31) As an experimental clone who possessed the pure DNA of the clone army's template, Jango, Omega was essential to Su's contingency plan.[[5]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-5) With their remaining supply of genetic samples taken from Fett continuing to degrade,[[31]](#cite_note-Replacements-31) Su intended to extract a sufficient amount of genetic material from Omega before terminating her. Se secretly undermined his efforts, however, using bounty hunter [Fennec Shand](/wiki/Fennec_Shand "Fennec Shand") to prevent the clone from being returned to Kamino by one of Su's mercenaries, such as [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane "Cad Bane").[[5]](#cite_note-Bounty_Lost-5)

 [![The Empire ended the production of clones on Kamino by destroying the planet's cloning facilities, including Tipoca City.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/TipocaCitySinks-KL.png/revision/latest?cb=20220119012742) [![The Empire ended the production of clones on Kamino by destroying the planet's cloning facilities, including Tipoca City.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/TipocaCitySinks-KL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220119012742)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2d/TipocaCitySinks-KL.png/revision/latest?cb=20220119012742) 

The Empire ended the production of clones on Kamino by destroying the planet's cloning facilities, including Tipoca City.

 

Having deemed the clone trooper program obsolete due to its cost,[[31]](#cite_note-Replacements-31) the Empire canceled its contracts with the Kaminoan government. [Vice Admiral](/wiki/Vice_Admiral "Vice Admiral") [Edmon Rampart](/wiki/Edmon_Rampart "Edmon Rampart") oversaw the [removal](/wiki/Attack_on_Kamino "Attack on Kamino") of all viable clones from Kamino, along with the Kaminoans' essential personnel and resources, putting the cloning technology firmly under the Empire's control. Prime Minister Su sought to evacuate his staff as well, hoping to continue his cloning operation elsewhere, but Rampart prevented him from succeeding and took Se into Imperial custody too since he and Tarkin believed she was still useful for the Empire due to her skills as the [Chief Medical Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Scientist "Chief Medical Scientist").[[32]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-32) Following the shutdown of clone production on Kamino, the [destruction of Tipoca City](/wiki/Rescue_of_Hunter "Rescue of Hunter") commenced when Rampart's [fleet](/wiki/Edmon_Rampart%27s_fleet "Edmon Rampart's fleet") of [*Venator*-class Star Destroyers](/wiki/Venator-class_Star_Destroyer "Venator-class Star Destroyer") opened fire on the decommissioned cloning facility after getting permission from Tarkin, the opening volleys causing large sections of the city to fall into the [ocean](/wiki/Ocean "Ocean").[[33]](#cite_note-Return_to_Kamino-33)

 [![The Galactic Empire turned the last generation of Fett clones into an expendable death squad.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/InquisitorTroopersHelmetless-2017DarthVader16.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180510032857) [![The Galactic Empire turned the last generation of Fett clones into an expendable death squad.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/InquisitorTroopersHelmetless-2017DarthVader16.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180510032857)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/InquisitorTroopersHelmetless-2017DarthVader16.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180510032857) 

The Galactic Empire turned the last generation of Fett clones into an expendable death squad.

 

The [final batches](/wiki/Purge_Trooper "Purge Trooper") were brought online,[[6]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_16-6) but the [Stormtrooper Corps](/wiki/Stormtrooper_Corps "Stormtrooper Corps") was henceforth comprised of [birth-born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") human volunteers[[34]](#cite_note-Propaganda-34) and children.[[29]](#cite_note-Stormtroopers-29) Under [Project War-Mantle](/wiki/Project_War-Mantle "Project War-Mantle"), the first members of the new generation of stormtroopers were recruited from across the galaxy and trained by [clone commandos](/wiki/Clone_commando "Clone commando") in an [Imperial base](/wiki/Imperial_Base_on_Daro "Imperial Base on Daro") on the planet [Daro](/wiki/Daro "Daro"). One of the recruiters, Commander [CC-5576](/wiki/Gregor "Gregor") "Gregor," noted that while the TK stormtroopers were not as skilled as clone troopers, they pledged their allegiance to the Empire whereas the clones were the soldiers of the Republic that no longer exists.[[32]](#cite_note-War-Mantle-32)

Although clones could be programmed for unconditional loyalty,[[13]](#cite_note-Episode_II-13) the Empire discovered that a more uniform, malleable soldier could be produced through the fervent patriotism of the young than the genetic duplication of a single template.[[34]](#cite_note-Propaganda-34) Boba Fett also survived the Clone Wars and became a notorious bounty hunter like his father before him.[[35]](#cite_note-CVD-35) While the relationship of Jango and Boba was that of donor and clone, Boba considered Jango his father.[[36]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-36)

 [![The Sith Eternal experimented with cloning as a way to preserve the essence of their master, Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/SithEternal-DB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200319155905) [![The Sith Eternal experimented with cloning as a way to preserve the essence of their master, Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/SithEternal-DB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200319155905)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/SithEternal-DB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200319155905) 

The Sith Eternal experimented with cloning as a way to preserve the essence of their master, Darth Sidious.

 

Secure in power as Emperor,[[37]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-37) Sidious employed his followers of the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal"), to help him obtain [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"). Based on the Sith’s hidden world [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"),[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) the cultists began to experiment with cloning[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) in a bid to extend the Sith Lord's lifespan and hopefully sustain it indefinitely;[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) should Sidious die, his soul would escape his body and take refuge in a cloned form.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) Kaminoan technology[[38]](#cite_note-Family_at_War-38) and Strand-Casting were used in the effort.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15)

The [Tarkin Initiative](/wiki/Tarkin_Initiative "Tarkin Initiative") utilized the genetic template of the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt") species to create a line of [Hutt clone troopers](/wiki/Hutt_clone_trooper "Hutt clone trooper"). The Empire possessed a small supply of Hutt clones, which were frozen in stasis aboard the [Hivebase-1](/wiki/Hivebase-1 "Hivebase-1") [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station"), having rejected them for mass production.[[39]](#cite_note-Aphra_18-39) Armed with [supercharged carbines](/wiki/Supercharged_carbine "Supercharged carbine"),[[9]](#cite_note-Aphra_19-9) the Hutt clones were [activated](/wiki/Infiltration_of_Hivebase-1 "Infiltration of Hivebase-1") by [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Yewl](/wiki/Yewl "Yewl") to serve as soldiers alongside his [personal guard](/wiki/Yewl%27s_guard "Yewl's guard") of [death troopers](/wiki/Death_trooper "Death trooper").[[39]](#cite_note-Aphra_18-39)

### New Republic Era[]

:   "*You are a clone. I've heard your voice thousands of times.*"
:   ―Bo-Katan Kryze, to Boba Fett[[36]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-36)

 [![Jango Fett's legacy survived through Boba Fett, an unaltered clone who he raised as his son.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/Chapter_4_The_Gathering_Storm.png/revision/latest?cb=20220119075931) [![Jango Fett's legacy survived through Boba Fett, an unaltered clone who he raised as his son.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/Chapter_4_The_Gathering_Storm.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220119075931)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/97/Chapter_4_The_Gathering_Storm.png/revision/latest?cb=20220119075931) 

Jango Fett's legacy survived through Boba Fett, an unaltered clone who he raised as his son.

 

Clones were remembered long after the Clone Wars, having made an impact on [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history "Timeline of galactic history"), well past the [fall of the Empire](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") and throughout the [era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era") of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic").[[34]](#cite_note-Propaganda-34) [Lady](/wiki/Lady "Lady") [Bo-Katan Kryze](/wiki/Bo-Katan_Kryze "Bo-Katan Kryze") recognized Boba by his clone origins, due to her [past dealings](/wiki/Siege_of_Mandalore "Siege of Mandalore") with the Republic and its clone army during the Clone Wars. She also knew that Fett's donor also provided the genetic material that spawned thousands of identical soldiers.[[36]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-36) During the days of the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era"), Commandant [Brendol Hux](/wiki/Brendol_Hux "Brendol Hux") who was a member of the [Shadow Council](/wiki/Shadow_Council_(Imperial_Remnants) "Shadow Council (Imperial Remnants)") of the [Imperial Remnants](/wiki/Imperial_Remnants "Imperial Remnants") [[40]](#cite_note-Chapter_23-40) and eventual First Order[[41]](#cite_note-Phasma-41) was incredibly interested in recreating and completing the lost cloning research for [Project Necromancer](/wiki/Project_Necromancer "Project Necromancer") of the [Imperial cloning program](/wiki/Imperial_cloning_program "Imperial cloning program") started by the late [Chief Scientist](/wiki/Chief_Scientist "Chief Scientist") [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor "Doctor") [Royce Hemlock](/wiki/Royce_Hemlock "Royce Hemlock") of the [Advanced Science Division](/wiki/Advanced_Science_Division "Advanced Science Division") of the [Imperial Science Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Science_Bureau "Imperial Science Bureau"). Fellow Shadow Council member [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Gideon](/wiki/Gideon "Gideon") decried it as an obsession while secretly doing his own cloning experiments.[[40]](#cite_note-Chapter_23-40)

 [![Through genetic experimentation, Moff Gideon's clones were imbued with the Force-sensitivity that the moff lacked.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/GideonsClones.png/revision/latest?cb=20241219035849) [![Through genetic experimentation, Moff Gideon's clones were imbued with the Force-sensitivity that the moff lacked.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/GideonsClones.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241219035849)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/GideonsClones.png/revision/latest?cb=20241219035849) 

Through genetic experimentation, Moff Gideon's clones were imbued with the Force-sensitivity that the moff lacked.

 

[Gideon's Imperial remnant](/wiki/Gideon%27s_Imperial_remnant "Gideon's Imperial remnant") employed the services of Doctor [Penn Pershing](/wiki/Penn_Pershing "Penn Pershing"), a clone engineer and a high-value target of the New Republic. Gideon tasked Pershing to oversee the remnant's experimentation on blood samples with a high count of [midi-chlorians](/wiki/Midi-chlorian "Midi-chlorian"). Pershing was captured by [Marshal](/wiki/Marshal "Marshal") [Carasynthia Dune](/wiki/Carasynthia_Dune "Carasynthia Dune") during the [Mandalorian warrior](/wiki/Mandalorian_warrior "Mandalorian warrior") [Din Djarin](/wiki/Din_Djarin "Din Djarin")'s efforts to [rescue](/wiki/Second_rescue_of_Grogu "Second rescue of Grogu") the [foundling](/wiki/Foundling "Foundling") [Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu").[[36]](#cite_note-Chapter_16-36) Although Pershing joined the [New Republic Amnesty Program](/wiki/New_Republic_Amnesty_Program "New Republic Amnesty Program"), the [Coruscant Accords](/wiki/Coruscant_Accords "Coruscant Accords") prevented him from continuing his research in cloning.[[42]](#cite_note-Chapter_19-42) Gideon had [Elia Kane](/wiki/Elia_Kane "Elia Kane") [erase](/wiki/Mind_Flayer "Mind Flayer") Pershing's memory to prevent him from leaking his clone project.[[40]](#cite_note-Chapter_23-40) Working from a hidden [Imperial base](/wiki/Mandalore_Imperial_base "Mandalore Imperial base") in the ruins of [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"), Gideon succeeded in creating a batch of clones that were modeled on his genetic template. Unlike their donor, however, [Gideon's clones](/wiki/Gideon%27s_clones "Gideon's clones") were [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") as a result of the moff's experimentation with genetic modification amidst the cloning process. Gideon's clones were destroyed by Djarin when Mandalorians [returned](/wiki/Conflict_on_Mandalore "Conflict on Mandalore") to their homeworld.[[43]](#cite_note-Chapter_24-43)

During the [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War"), the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") had an argument with his rival and Brendol’s son, [General](/wiki/General "General") [Armitage Hux](/wiki/Armitage_Hux "Armitage Hux"), concerning the [newest generation of stormtroopers](/wiki/First_Order_stormtrooper "First Order stormtrooper"). Ren openly criticized Hux's soldiers, convinced they were all capable of high treason due to the [actions](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Finalizer "Escape from the Finalizer") of a [single traitor](/wiki/Finn "Finn") in their ranks, and declared [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") should consider using a clone army.[[44]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-44)

### Darth Sidious reborn[]

#### The Emperor's cloned body[]

:   "*As the Empire perished, I was born again, my consciousness transferred into a new body on Exegol. Alas, even after years of experimentation, the cloning techniques employed by my acolytes were inadequate. They could not create a vessel capable of containing my unfathomable power.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15)

After a generation of Sith rule over the galaxy,[[45]](#cite_note-DBPalpatine-45) Darth Sidious got killed by his [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice"), Sith warlord [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), who gave his life to save his son, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker").[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-46) With their deaths, the lineage of Sith from [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane") to Vader was broken.[[47]](#cite_note-TLJ:TVD-47) Anakin fulfilled his destiny as the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") by bringing balance to the Force,[[48]](#cite_note-Luke_Skywalker-48) but Sidious had discovered a way to return from death.[[45]](#cite_note-DBPalpatine-45)

 [![Darth Sidious cheated death by transferring his spirit into a clone of himself.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/Palpatine_returning-TROSAdaptation1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250301043617) [![Darth Sidious cheated death by transferring his spirit into a clone of himself.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/Palpatine_returning-TROSAdaptation1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250301043617)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/Palpatine_returning-TROSAdaptation1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250301043617) 

Darth Sidious cheated death by transferring his spirit into a clone of himself.

 

Darth Sidious died when his body was destroyed on the [DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station")'s [main reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") during the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor")[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16)[[46]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-46) in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY").[[49]](#cite_note-GA-49) However, his spirit passed into a clone that had been hastily prepared on Exegol[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17). Using the knowledge gained from his Master [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis"), Sidious succeeded in transferring his essence to his clone,[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16) but the process was rushed and flawed. While Sidious sensed a remnant of the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force") within Vader and suspected his apprentice’s loyalty was not where it lied before the Empire rose to power, he did not foresee that Vader would turn against him at [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor").[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17)

Darth Sidious' clone was deemed an imperfect replacement, suffering from physical deterioration as a result of his powerful connection to the dark side. The Sith Eternal [cult](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult") attempted to perfect the procedure that led to the Sith Lord's revival. They conducted many experiments on his genetic template, creating multiple specimens through the process of [gene](/wiki/Gene "Gene") splicing, but none of their creations were deemed a suitable replacement to Sidious' current vessel. Although his clone was wracked with pain, the Emperor sought to prolong its survival by relying on Clone War-era technology and an ancient [Ommin harness](/wiki/Ommin_harness "Ommin harness").[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17)

#### The creation of Snoke[]

:   "*As part of their genetic experiments, my followers had attempted to create another being that came to be known as Snoke. Although his body proved unworthy of containing my dark essence, Snoke's natural sensitivity to the Force would make him a powerful puppet nonetheless.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15)

 [![Snoke was an artificial strandcast constructed from the genetic template of Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Strandcast_Snoke.png/revision/latest?cb=20211106034814) [![Snoke was an artificial strandcast constructed from the genetic template of Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Strandcast_Snoke.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211106034814)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Strandcast_Snoke.png/revision/latest?cb=20211106034814) 

Snoke was an artificial strandcast constructed from the genetic template of Darth Sidious.

 

The Sith Eternal conducted more experiments with Darth Sidious' genetic template, endeavoring to create a stronger vessel to contain their master's essence unlike the flawed clone that he inhabited. One of the specimens that they engineered was naturally intoned with the Force; however, the Sith Lord deemed it an "unworthy" form. Nevertheless, he saw its usefulness as a figurehead through which he could influence galactic events from his [sanctuary](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel") on Exegol.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) This being adopted the identity of Snoke,[[50]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_2-50) becoming the Supreme Leader of the First Order.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) Although Snoke was capable of self-determination,[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) his actions and objectives were influenced by Sidious[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) and the Sith Eternal.[[37]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-37) In addition to taking control of the First Order,[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) Snoke's creators designed him to train Ren, the [grandson](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") of Darth Vader, as an heir to the new[[37]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-37) [Sith Empire](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order")[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4) the Sith Eternal secretly created in the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions").[[37]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-37)

#### The son of Darth Sidious[]

:   "*Using a technique known as Strand-Casting, countless modified clone bodies were produced from my genetic template. All but one of them were utter failures. The lone subject that survived the cloning process lacked any connection to the Force.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15)

 [![An offshoot of the Sith Eternal's genetic experiments, Darth Sidious' son sired a Force-sensitive child called Rey.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Reys_Parents.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200825042956) [![An offshoot of the Sith Eternal's genetic experiments, Darth Sidious' son sired a Force-sensitive child called Rey.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Reys_Parents.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200825042956)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/70/Reys_Parents.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200825042956) 

An offshoot of the Sith Eternal's genetic experiments, Darth Sidious' son sired a Force-sensitive child called Rey.

 

Despite years of experience in cloning, the Sith Eternal continually failed to create a stable host for Sidious' spirit. Using a form of cloning known as Strand-Casting, they engineered multiple specimens from Sidious' template, none of which were considered a success. Only one of their creations survived the cloning process;[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) a byproduct of the Sith Eternal's genetic experiments, the Emperor's "son" had been engineered from his cloned tissue, as well as other genetic samples,[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16) during the Imperial Era.[[8]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-8) The result had been a healthy strandcast instead of an exact clone of Sidious.[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17) While Sidious regarded the strandcast as his son from a biological standpoint, he noted with disappointment that the strandcast lacked any connection to the Force.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) The Emperor's son was a healthy, yet ordinary man,[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17) and as such, he rejected what he saw as a "useless creature."[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15)

Though appalled by his son's lack of Force-sensitivity, Sidious permitted the strandcast to live in order to preserve the [Palpatine family](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family") through natural methods, having theorized the next generation could inherit his power.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15) When Vader and [Ochi of Bestoon](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi") journeyed to Exegol, the clone took the chance to escape and lived away from his father ever since, taking the name Dathan after a [Sith slave](/wiki/Dathan_(Symeong) "Dathan (Symeong)") who helped him.[[8]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-8) Sidious' plan succeeded when the strandcast sired Rey, who was Force-sensitive like her grandfather. While the Sith Lord did not anticipate his son's relationship with [Rey's mother](/wiki/Miramir "Miramir"),[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17) he was determined to take possession of their child nonetheless.[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16) Sidious regarded her as another heir to the new Sith Empire and the only vessel capable of housing his spirit. Rey's father, however, fled into hiding with his child and her mother, disrupting the Emperor's plan for Rey.[[15]](#cite_note-SotS-15)

#### Return of the Emperor[]

:   "*It cannot be. The Emperor is dead.*"  
    "*Dark science. Cloning. Secrets only the Sith knew.*"
:   ―Aftab Ackbar and Beaumont Kin[[51]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-51)

 [![Darth Sidious planned to possess his granddaughter to escape his clone.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/Transference.png/revision/latest?cb=20211106230753) [![Darth Sidious planned to possess his granddaughter to escape his clone.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/Transference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211106230753)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/Transference.png/revision/latest?cb=20211106230753) 

Darth Sidious planned to possess his granddaughter to escape his clone.

 

Darth Sidious' clone was on the verge of death by the time he [broadcasted](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_broadcast "Palpatine's broadcast") his return to the galaxy during the [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War"). His flesh became putrid; he was blind in both [eyes](/wiki/Eye "Eye"); and completely dependent on the support of his harness for survival. Supreme Leader Ren estimated only a short time remained before Sidious' clone was completely destroyed by his connection to the dark side.[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17) In addition to finding the Sith Lord on Exegol, Ren discovered the genetic duplicates of Snoke, who were kept sedated in a tank of nutrient fluid.[[4]](#cite_note-TSWB-4)

Sidious' return baffled [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") [Aftab Ackbar](/wiki/Aftab_Ackbar "Aftab Ackbar"), [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Rose Tico](/wiki/Rose_Tico "Rose Tico"), and other members of the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance").[[51]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-51) Sidious was believed to have been dead by this time.[[45]](#cite_note-DBPalpatine-45) However, [Resistance trooper](/wiki/Resistance_trooper "Resistance trooper") [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Beaumont Kin](/wiki/Beaumont_Kin "Beaumont Kin") correctly[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17) theorized Hemlock’s dark cloning science was involved in the Emperor's revival as well as secrets only the Sith knew.[[51]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-51) As Darth Sidious' plot for revenge continued apace, Rey [confronted](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") her grandfather on Exegol where she learned the details of his survival through cloning in a [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision"). The Sith Lord goaded Rey to surrender herself to the dark side by participating in a [ritual sacrifice](/wiki/Transference "Transference"). By killing Sidious in anger and hatred, Rey would become possessed by his spirit, freeing him from the confine of his cloned vessel.[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17)

 [![Darth Sidious perished with the destruction of cloned body during the Battle of Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/The_death_of_Sidious.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401233403) [![Darth Sidious perished with the destruction of cloned body during the Battle of Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/The_death_of_Sidious.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401233403)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/The_death_of_Sidious.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401233403) 

Darth Sidious perished with the destruction of cloned body during the Battle of Exegol.

 

Rey's youth, her strength in the Force, and her lineage made her the most suitable host in the Emperor's mind. While his plan relied on her ending the existence of his cloned body, Sidious was content to know that their souls would be merged within her body,[[16]](#cite_note-Skywalker:_A_Family_at_War-16) allowing him to rule the galaxy in spirit.[[45]](#cite_note-DBPalpatine-45) However, the Sith Lord abandoned this plan upon discovering the extent of Rey's [Force-bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") with Solo, who renounced the dark persona of Kylo Ren. The realization that they were a [dyad in the Force](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad") led Sidious to drain them of their combined power, thereby healing his body and restoring himself to full power. Vowing to herald the return of the Sith, Sidious moved to annihilate the Resistance but was opposed by Rey, who managed to destroy his spirit's vessel with the help of all the Jedi who were [one with the Force](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit").[[17]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-17)
